List the properties you need to query. } else {$True} }] [string]$SelectProperties, [ParameterMandatory = $false] [AliasF] [string]$Filter, [ParameterMandatory = $false] [AliasR] [bool]$Rewindable = $false, [ParameterMandatory = $false] [AliasT] [int]$QueryTimeoutSeconds = 3 $managementScope = New-Object System.Management.ManagementScope$WmiNameSpace $options = New-Object System.Management.EnumerationOptions $options.EnumerateDeep = $true $options.ReturnImmediately = $true $options.Rewindable = $Rewindable $options.Timeout = New-TimeSpan -Seconds $QueryTimeoutSeconds $filterClause = if $Filter -and -not $Filter.ToLower.StartsWithwhere { $filterClause = WHERE $Filter } $queryString = SELECT $SelectProperties FROM $WmiClass$filterClause New-Object System.Management.ManagementObjectSearcher $managementScope, $queryString, $options.Get } $Caption = Get-WmiInformation -WmiClass win32_operatingsystem -SelectProperties Caption.Caption If $Caption -like *server* { N/A on Server OS Exit } if $Caption -like *windows 11* { N/A on Windows 11 Exit } if $PSVersionTable.PSVersion -lt [Version]5.1 { Write-Output Undetermined|This script requires PowerShell 5.1 or later Exit } #============================================================================================================================= # # Description: Verifies the hardware compliance.
